--- Commit Message ---
LU-18562 osd: llog write batch block allocation

as we need to grab a semaphore to serialize block allocation,
it makes sense to allocate few blocks at once.

todo:
 - optimization: save last used bhs in osd object
 - concurrent append vs read test

Here's summary of my changes:
The change in this patch replaces the deprecated `cfs_kernel_write()` function with the newer `kernel_write()` function in the `llog_test_11` function. 

### Summary of Changes:
- **Old function**: `cfs_kernel_write(filp, buf, 2, &filp->f_pos)`
- **New function**: `kernel_write(filp, buf, 2, &filp->f_pos)`

### Purpose:
This update fixes a compile error caused by the use of an obsolete or removed `cfs_kernel_write` function, which was part of the older CFS (Computing Framework Subsystem) layer. The `kernel_write` function is the standard, maintained kernel API for writing data to a file descriptor from kernel space.

### Impact:
- Ensures the code compiles successfully.
- Aligns with current kernel coding practices by using the standard `kernel_write` interface.
- Maintains functionality: writes the string "3\n" to `/proc/sys/vm/drop_caches` to trigger cache dropping, as part of the test.
